FNV FINAL RENDERER SUN/LIGHT COLOR CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which shader constant registrations carry final light color/direction data?
2. Are LightColors / Diffuse Light color backed by renderer globals or per-material object fields?
3. Which code writes the backing globals before BSShader::SetShaders?
4. Is there a renderer-owned PSY_SunColor source independent of the rejected Sun +0x1C/Main +0x1C alias?

Expected use:
Prefer final shader constant backing stores if this proves writer ownership and lifetime. Do not use Reloaded's rejected Sun/Main directional-light alias.
